<section id="python-sdk">
<span id="sdk"></span>
<h1 id="python-sdk">Python SDK<a href="#python-sdk" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this heading">#</a></h1>
<p>The SDK is best for writing Python scripts to interact with your
RedBrick AI organization &amp; projects. The SDK offers granular
functions for programmatically manipulating data, importing annotations,
assigning tasks, and more.</p>
<section id="module-redbrick">
<span id="redbrick"></span>
<h2 id="redbrick">RedBrick<a href="#module-redbrick" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this heading">#</a></h2>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-prename descclassname"><span
class="pre">redbrick.</span></span><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">StorageMethod</span></span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/storage.html#StorageMethod"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a href="#redbrick.StorageMethod"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Storage method integration for organizations.</p>
<ul>
<li><dl>
<dt><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">PUBLIC</code></span> - Access files
from a public cloud storage service using their absolute URLs.</dt>
<dd>
<p>(i.e. files available publicly)</p>
</dd>
</dl></li>
<li><dl>
<dt><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">REDBRICK</code></span> - Access
files stored on RedBrick AI’s servers</dt>
<dd>
<p>(i.e. files uploaded directly to RBAI from a local machine)</p>
</dd>
</dl></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">Public</span></span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/storage.html#StorageMethod.Public"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.StorageMethod.Public" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Public storage provider (Sub class of <a
href="#redbrick.StorageProvider" class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.StorageProvider"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">StorageProvider</code></span></a>).</p>
<dl>

class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">access_key_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">secret_access_key</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">role_arn</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">role_external_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span

class="pre">session_duration</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">3600</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/storage.html#StorageMethod.AWSS3.Details"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.StorageMethod.AWSS3.Details" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>AWS S3 storage provider details.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Variables<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>bucket</strong> (<em>str</em>) – AWS S3 bucket.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>region</strong> (<em>str</em>) – AWS S3 region.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>transfer_acceleration</strong> (<em>bool</em>) – AWS S3
transfer acceleration.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>endpoint</strong> (<em>str</em>) – Custom endpoint (For
S3 compatible storage, e.g. MinIO).</p></li>
<li><p><strong>access_key_id</strong> (<em>str</em>) – AWS access key
id.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>secret_access_key</strong> (<em>str</em>) – AWS secret
access key. (Will be None in output for security reasons)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>role_arn</strong> (<em>str</em>) – AWS assume_role ARN.
(For short-lived credentials instead of access keys)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>role_external_id</strong> (<em>str</em>) – AWS
assume_role external id. (Will be None in output for security
reasons)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>session_duration</strong> (<em>int</em>) – AWS S3
assume_role session duration.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>

<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-prename descclassname"><span
class="pre">redbrick.</span></span><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">TaskEventTypes</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">value</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">names=&lt;not</span> <span
class="pre">given&gt;</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">*values</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">module=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">qualname=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">type=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">start=1</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">boundary=None</span></span></em><span
class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/enums.html#TaskEventTypes"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a href="#redbrick.TaskEventTypes"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Enumerate the different types of task events.</p>
<ul>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_CREATED</code></span> - A new
task has been created.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_SUBMITTED</code></span> - A
task has been submitted for review.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_ACCEPTED</code></span> - A
submitted task has been accepted in review.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_REJECTED</code></span> - A
submitted task has been rejected in review.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_CORRECTED</code></span> - A
submitted task has been corrected in review.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_ASSIGNED</code></span> - A
task has been assigned to a worker.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_REASSIGNED</code></span> - A
task has been reassigned to another worker.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_UNASSIGNED</code></span> - A
task has been unassigned from a worker.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_SKIPPED</code></span> - A task
has been skipped by a worker.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">TASK_SAVED</code></span> - A task
has been saved but not yet submitted.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">GROUNDTRUTH_TASK_EDITED</code></span>
- A ground truth task has been edited.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">CONSENSUS_COMPUTED</code></span> -
The consensus for a task has been computed.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">COMMENT_ADDED</code></span> - A
comment has been added to a task.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">CONSENSUS_TASK_EDITED</code></span>
- A consensus task has been edited.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-prename descclassname"><span
class="pre">redbrick.</span></span><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">TaskFilters</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">value</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">names=&lt;not</span> <span
class="pre">given&gt;</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">*values</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">module=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">qualname=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">type=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">start=1</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">boundary=None</span></span></em><span
class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/enums.html#TaskFilters"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a href="#redbrick.TaskFilters"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Enumerate the different task filters.</p>
<ul>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">ALL</code></span> - All
tasks.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">GROUNDTRUTH</code></span> - Ground
truth tasks only.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">UNASSIGNED</code></span> - Tasks
that have not yet been assigned to a worker.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">QUEUED</code></span> - Tasks that
are queued for labeling/review.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">DRAFT</code></span> - Tasks that
have been saved as draft.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">SKIPPED</code></span> - Tasks that
have been skipped by a worker.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">COMPLETED</code></span> - Tasks
that have been completed successfully.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">FAILED</code></span> - Tasks that
have been rejected in review.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">ISSUES</code></span> - Tasks that
have issues raised and cannot be completed.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-prename descclassname"><span
class="pre">redbrick.</span></span><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">TaskStates</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">value</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">names=&lt;not</span> <span
class="pre">given&gt;</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">*values</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">module=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">qualname=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">type=None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">start=1</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">boundary=None</span></span></em><span
class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/enums.html#TaskStates"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a href="#redbrick.TaskStates"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Task Status.</p>
<ul>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">UNASSIGNED</code></span> - The Task
has not been assigned to a Project Admin or Member.</p></li>
<li><dl>
<dt><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">ASSIGNED</code></span> - The Task
has been assigned to a Project Admin or Member,</dt>
<dd>
<p>but work has not begun on it.</p>
</dd>
</dl></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">IN_PROGRESS</code></span> - The
Task is currently being worked on by a Project Admin or Member.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">COMPLETED</code></span> - The Task
has been completed successfully.</p></li>
<li><dl>
<dt><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">PROBLEM</code></span> - A Project
Admin or Member has raised an Issue regarding the Task,</dt>
<dd>
<p>and work cannot continue until the Issue is resolved by a Project
Admin.</p>
</dd>
</dl></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">SKIPPED</code></span> - The Task
has been skipped.</p></li>
<li><p><span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">STAGED</code></span> - The Task has
been saved as a Draft.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>

<p>Label Stage.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>stage_name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – Stage name.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>on_submit</strong> (<em>Union[bool,</em> <em>str]</em>
<em>= True</em>) – The next stage for the task when submitted in current
stage. If True, the task will go to ground truth. If False, the task
will be archived.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>config</strong> (<em>Config = Config()</em>) – Stage
config.</p></li>

class="pre">show_uploaded_annotations</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span

class="o"><span class="pre">=</span></span><span

class="o"><span class="pre">=</span></span><span
class="default_value"><span class="pre">None</span></span></em>,

title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Label Stage Config.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>auto_assignment</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em>) –
Enable task auto assignment. (Default: True)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>auto_assignment_queue_size</strong>
(<em>Optional[int]</em>) – Task auto-assignment queue size. (Default:
5)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>show_uploaded_annotations</strong>
(<em>Optional[bool]</em>) – Show uploaded annotations to users.
(Default: True)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>read_only_labels_edit_access</strong>
(<em>Optional[</em><a href="#redbrick.ProjectMember.Role"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.ProjectMember.Role"><em>ProjectMember.Role</em></a><em>]</em>)
– Access level to change the read only labels. (Default: None)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>is_pre_label</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em>) – Is
pre-labeling stage. (Default: False)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>is_consensus_label</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em>) –
Is consensus-labeling stage. (Default: False)</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>

<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span

class="pre">ReviewStage</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">stage_name</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">config=&lt;factory&gt;</span></span></em>, <em><span
class="n"><span class="pre">on_accept=True</span></span></em>, <em><span
class="n"><span class="pre">on_reject=False</span></span></em><span
class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/stage/review.html#ReviewStage"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a href="#redbrick.ReviewStage"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Review Stage.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>stage_name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – Stage name.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>on_accept</strong> (<em>Union[bool,</em> <em>str]</em>
<em>= True</em>) – The next stage for the task when accepted in current
stage. If True, the task will go to ground truth. If False, the task
will be archived.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>on_reject</strong> (<em>Union[bool,</em> <em>str]</em>
<em>= False</em>) – The next stage for the task when rejected in current
stage. If True, the task will go to ground truth. If False, the task
will be archived.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>config</strong> (<em>Config = Config()</em>) – Stage
config.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">Config</span></span><span

class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">auto_assignment</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">auto_assignment_queue_size</span></span><span
class="o"><span class="pre">=</span></span><span
class="default_value"><span class="pre">None</span></span></em>,
<em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">read_only_labels_edit_access</span></span><span
class="o"><span class="pre">=</span></span><span
class="default_value"><span class="pre">None</span></span></em>,
<em><span class="n"><span class="pre">is_pre_review</span></span><span
class="o"><span class="pre">=</span></span><span
class="default_value"><span class="pre">None</span></span></em>,
<em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">is_consensus_merge</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/stage/review.html#ReviewStage.Config"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.ReviewStage.Config" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Review Stage Config.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>review_percentage</strong> (<em>Optional[float]</em>) –
Percentage of tasks in [0, 1] that will be sampled for review. (Default:
1)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>auto_assignment</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em>) –
Enable task auto assignment. (Default: True)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>auto_assignment_queue_size</strong>
(<em>Optional[int]</em>) – Task auto-assignment queue size. (Default:
5)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>read_only_labels_edit_access</strong>
(<em>Optional[</em><a href="#redbrick.ProjectMember.Role"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.ProjectMember.Role"><em>ProjectMember.Role</em></a><em>]</em>)
– Access level to change the read only labels. (Default: None)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>is_pre_review</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em>) – Is
pre-review stage. (Default: False)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>is_consensus_merge</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em>) –
Is consensus-merge (V2) stage. (Default: False)</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>

class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a href="#redbrick.get_org"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Get an existing redbrick organization object.</p>
<p>Organization object allows you to interact with your organization and
perform high level actions like creating a project.</p>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; org = redbrick.get_org(org_id, api_key)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>org_id</strong> (<em>str</em>) – Your organizations
unique id <a href="https://app.redbrickai.com"
class="reference external">https://app.redbrickai.com</a>/&lt;org_id&gt;/.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>api_key</strong> (<em>str</em>) – Your secret api_key,
can be created from the RedBrick AI platform.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>url</strong> (<em>str = DEFAULT_URL</em>) – Should
default to <a href="https://api.redbrickai.com"
class="reference external">https://api.redbrickai.com</a></p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>

</dd>
</dl>
</dd>

<section id="organization">
<span id="org"></span>
<h2 id="organization">Organization<a href="#organization"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this heading">#</a></h2>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-prename descclassname"><span
class="pre">redbrick.</span></span><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">RBOrganization</span></span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/entities.html#RBOrganization"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a href="#redbrick.RBOrganization"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Bases: <span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">ABC</code></span></p>
<p>Representation of RedBrick organization.</p>
<p>The <a href="#redbrick.RBOrganization" class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.RBOrganization"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">redbrick.RBOrganization</code></span></a>
object allows you to programmatically interact with your RedBrick
organization. This class provides methods for querying your organization
and doing other high level actions. Retrieve the organization object in
the following way:</p>
<dl>
<dt>Variables<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>team</strong> (<a href="#redbrick.common.member.Team"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.common.member.Team"><em>redbrick.common.member.Team</em></a>)
– Organization team management.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>storage</strong> (<a
href="#redbrick.common.storage.Storage" class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.common.storage.Storage"><em>redbrick.common.storage.Storage</em></a>)
– Organization storage methods integration.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; org = redbrick.get_org(org_id=&quot;&quot;, api_key=&quot;&quot;)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w"> </span><span
class="pre">property</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">org_id</span></span><em><span class="p"><span
class="pre">:</span></span><span class="w"> </span><span
class="pre">str</span></em><a href="#redbrick.RBOrganization.org_id"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Retrieve the unique org_id of this organization.</p>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w"> </span><span

<dd>
<p>Create a workspace within the organization.</p>
<p>This method creates a worspace in a similar fashion to the quickstart
on the RedBrick AI create workspace page.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – A unique name for your
workspace</p></li>
<li><p><strong>exists_okay</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Allow
workspaces with the same name to be returned instead of trying to create
a new workspace. Useful for when running the same script repeatedly when
you do not want to keep creating new workspaces.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>A RedBrick Workspace object.</p>

<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">create_project_advanced</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">name</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">taxonomy_name</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">stages</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">exists_okay</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">workspace_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">sibling_tasks</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">consensus_settings</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/entities.html#RBOrganization.create_project_advanced"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.RBOrganization.create_project_advanced"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Create a project within the organization.</p>
<p>This method creates a project in a similar fashion to the quickstart
on the RedBrick AI create project page.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – A unique name for your
project</p></li>
<li><p><strong>taxonomy_name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – The name of the
taxonomy you want to use for this project. Taxonomies can be found on
the left side bar of the platform.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>stages</strong> (<em>List[</em><a href="#redbrick.Stage"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.Stage"><em>Stage</em></a><em>]</em>) – List of stage
configs.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>exists_okay</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Allow
projects with the same name to be returned instead of trying to create a
new project. Useful for when running the same script repeatedly when you
do not want to keep creating new projects.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>workspace_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – The id of the workspace that you want to add this project
to.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>sibling_tasks</strong> (<em>Optional[int]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Number of tasks created for each uploaded
datapoint.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>consensus_settings</strong> (<em>Optional[Dict[str,</em>
<em>Any]]</em> <em>= None</em>) –</p>
<dl>
<dt>Consensus settings for the project. It has keys:</dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p>minAnnotations: int</p></li>
<li><p>autoAcceptThreshold?: float (range [0, 1])</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>A RedBrick Project object.</p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p><a href="#redbrick.RBProject" class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.RBProject">redbrick.RBProject</a></p>
</dd>
<dt>Raises<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p><strong>ValueError:</strong> – If a project with the same name exists
but has a different type or taxonomy.</p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">create_project</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">name</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">taxonomy_name</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">reviews</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">0</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">exists_okay</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">workspace_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">sibling_tasks</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">consensus_settings</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/entities.html#RBOrganization.create_project"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.RBOrganization.create_project" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Create a project within the organization.</p>
<p>This method creates a project in a similar fashion to the quickstart
on the RedBrick AI create project page.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – A unique name for your
project</p></li>
<li><p><strong>taxonomy_name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – The name of the
taxonomy you want to use for this project. Taxonomies can be found on
the left side bar of the platform.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>reviews</strong> (<em>int = 0</em>) – The number of
review stages that you want to add after the label stage.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>exists_okay</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Allow
projects with the same name to be returned instead of trying to create a
new project. Useful for when running the same script repeatedly when you
do not want to keep creating new projects.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>workspace_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – The id of the workspace that you want to add this project
to.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>sibling_tasks</strong> (<em>Optional[int]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Number of tasks created for each uploaded
datapoint.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>consensus_settings</strong> (<em>Optional[Dict[str,</em>
<em>Any]]</em> <em>= None</em>) –</p>
<dl>
<dt>Consensus settings for the project. It has keys:</dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p>minAnnotations: int</p></li>
<li><p>autoAcceptThreshold?: float (range [0, 1])</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>A RedBrick Project object.</p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p><a href="#redbrick.RBProject" class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.RBProject">redbrick.RBProject</a></p>
</dd>
<dt>Raises<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p><strong>ValueError:</strong> – If a project with the same name exists
but has a different type or taxonomy.</p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>

class="sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python"><span class="bu">str</span></code></span></span>)
– Unique identifier for the taxonomy.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>study_classify</strong> (<span
class="sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">Optional</code></span>[<span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">List</code></span>[<a
href="formats/taxonomy.html#redbrick.types.taxonomy.Attribute"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.types.taxonomy.Attribute"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">Attribute</code></span></a>]]</span>) – Study
level classification applies to the task.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>series_classify</strong> (<span
class="sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">Optional</code></span>[<span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">List</code></span>[<a
href="formats/taxonomy.html#redbrick.types.taxonomy.Attribute"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.types.taxonomy.Attribute"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">Attribute</code></span></a>]]</span>) – Series
level classification applies to a single series within a task.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>instance_classify</strong> (<span
class="sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">Optional</code></span>[<span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">List</code></span>[<a
href="formats/taxonomy.html#redbrick.types.taxonomy.Attribute"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.types.taxonomy.Attribute"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">Attribute</code></span></a>]]</span>) –
Instance classification applies to a single frame (video) or slice (3D
volume).</p></li>
<li><p><strong>object_types</strong> (<span
class="sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">Optional</code></span>[<span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">List</code></span>[<a
href="formats/taxonomy.html#redbrick.types.taxonomy.ObjectType"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.types.taxonomy.ObjectType"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">ObjectType</code></span></a>]]</span>) –
Object types are used to annotate features/objects in tasks, for
example, segmentation or bounding boxes.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>

<dd>

<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">create_datapoints</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">storage_id</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">points</span></span></em>, <em><span class="o"><span
class="pre">*</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">50</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/entities.html#RBWorkspace.create_datapoints"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.RBWorkspace.create_datapoints" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Create datapoints in workspace.</p>
<p>Upload data to your workspace (without annotations). Please visit <a
href="https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#import"
class="reference external">our documentation</a> to understand the
format for <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">points</code></span>.</p>
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>workspace = redbrick.get_workspace(org_id, workspace_id, api_key, url)
points = [
    {
        &quot;name&quot;: &quot;...&quot;,
        &quot;series&quot;: [
            {
                &quot;items&quot;: &quot;...&quot;,
            }
        ]
    }
]
workspace.create_datapoints(storage_id, points)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>storage_id</strong> (<em>str</em>) – Your RedBrick AI
external storage_id. This can be found under the Storage Tab on the
RedBrick AI platform. To directly upload images to rbai, use
redbrick.StorageMethod.REDBRICK.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>points</strong> (List[<a
href="formats/index.html#redbrick.types.task.InputTask"
class="reference internal" title="redbrick.types.task.InputTask"><span
class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">InputTask</code></span></a>]) – Please see the
RedBrick AI reference documentation for overview of the format. <a
href="https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#import"
class="reference external">https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#import</a>.
Fields with annotation information are not supported in
workspace.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 50</em>) –</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>List of datapoint objects with key response if successful, else
error</p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>List[Dict]</p>
</dd>
</dl>
<div class="admonition note">
<p>Note</p>
<p>1. If doing direct upload, please use <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">redbrick.StorageMethod.REDBRICK</code></span>
as the storage id. Your items path must be a valid path to a locally
stored image.</p>
<p>2. When doing direct upload i.e. <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">redbrick.StorageMethod.REDBRICK</code></span>,
if you didn’t specify a “name” field in your datapoints object, we will
assign the “items” path to it.</p>
</div>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">update_datapoints_metadata</span></span><span

points = [
    {
        &quot;dpId&quot;: &quot;...&quot;,
        &quot;metaData&quot;: {
            &quot;property&quot;: &quot;value&quot;,
        }
    }
]

datapoints with dpId and metaData values.</p></li>

<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">delete_datapoints</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">dp_ids</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span

href="_modules/redbrick/common/entities.html#RBWorkspace.delete_datapoints"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.RBWorkspace.delete_datapoints" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Delete workspace datapoints based on ids.</p>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; workspace = redbrick.get_workspace(org_id, workspace_id, api_key, url)
&gt;&gt;&gt; workspace.delete_datapoints([...])</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>dp_ids</strong> (<em>List[str]</em>) – List of datapoint
ids to delete.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 50</em>) – The number of
datapoints to delete at a time. We recommend keeping this &lt;=
50.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>True if successful, else False.</p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>bool</p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>

class="pre">[</span></span><span class="pre">str</span><span
class="p"><span class="pre">,</span></span><span class="w"> </span><span
class="pre">str</span><span class="p"><span
class="pre">]</span></span></em><a
href="#redbrick.RBProject.label_storage" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Read only label_storage property.</p>
<p>Retrieves the label storage id and path.</p>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w"> </span><span

<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">set_label_storage</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">storage_id</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">path</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/entities.html#RBProject.set_label_storage"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.RBProject.set_label_storage" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Set label storage method for a project.</p>
<p>By default, all annotations get stored in RedBrick AI’s storage i.e.
<span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">redbrick.StorageMethod.REDBRICK</code></span>.
Set a custom external storage, within which RedBrick AI will write all
annotations.</p>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; project = redbrick.get_project(org_id, project_id, api_key)
&gt;&gt;&gt; project.set_label_storage(storage_id)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>storage_id</strong> (<em>str</em>) – The unique ID of
your RedBrick AI storage method integration. Found on the storage method
tab on the left sidebar.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>path</strong> (<em>str</em>) – A prefix path within which
the annotations will be written.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>Returns [storage_id, path]</p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>Tuple[str, str]</p>
</dd>
</dl>
<div class="admonition important">
<p>Important</p>
<p>You only need to run this command once per project.</p>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Raises<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p><strong>ValueError:</strong> – If there are validation errors.</p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">

class="pre">update_stage</span></span><span

<h2 id="export">Export<a href="#export" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this heading">#</a></h2>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-prename descclassname"><span
class="pre">redbrick.common.export.</span></span><span
class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">Export</span></span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/export.html#Export"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.export.Export" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Bases: <span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">ABC</code></span></p>
<p>Primary interface for various export methods.</p>
<p>The export module has many functions for exporting annotations and
meta-data from projects. The export module is available from the <a
href="#redbrick.RBProject" class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.RBProject"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">redbrick.RBProject</code></span></a>
module.</p>
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; project = redbrick.get_project(api_key=&quot;&quot;, org_id=&quot;&quot;, project_id=&quot;&quot;)
&gt;&gt;&gt; project.export # Export</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">export_tasks</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="o"><span
class="pre">*</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">10</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">only_ground_truth</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">stage_name</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">task_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">from_timestamp</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">old_format</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">without_masks</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">without_json</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">semantic_mask</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">binary_mask</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">no_consensus</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">with_files</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">dicom_to_nifti</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">png</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">rt_struct</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">mhd</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">destination</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/export.html#Export.export_tasks"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.export.Export.export_tasks" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Export annotation data.</p>
<p>Meta-data and category information returned as an Object.
Segmentations are written to your disk in NIfTI-1 format. Please <a
href="https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#export"
class="reference external">visit our documentation</a> for more
information on the format.</p>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; project = redbrick.get_project(org_id, project_id, api_key, url)
&gt;&gt;&gt; project.export.export_tasks()</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 10</em>) –</p></li>
<li><p><strong>only_ground_truth</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – If
set to True, will only return data that has been completed in your
workflow. If False, will export latest state.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>stage_name</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – If set, will only export tasks that are currently in the
given stage.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>task_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>= None</em>)
– If the unique task_id is mentioned, only a single datapoint will be
exported.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>from_timestamp</strong> (<em>Optional[float]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – If the timestamp is mentioned, will only export tasks that
were labeled/updated since the given timestamp. Format - output from
datetime.timestamp()</p></li>
<li><p><strong>old_format</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Whether to
export tasks in old format.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>without_masks</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Exports
only tasks JSON without downloading any segmentation masks. Note: This
is not recommended for tasks with overlapping labels.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>without_json</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Doesn’t
create the tasks JSON file.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>semantic_mask</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Whether
to export all segmentations as semantic_mask. This will create one
instance per class. If this is set to True and a task has multiple
instances per class, then attributes belonging to each instance will not
be exported.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>binary_mask</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Whether to export all segmentations as binary masks. This
will create one segmentation file per instance. If this is set to None
and a task has overlapping labels, then binary_mask option will be True
for that particular task.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>no_consensus</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Whether to export tasks without consensus info. If None,
will default to export with consensus info, if it is enabled for the
given project. (Applicable only for new format export)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>with_files</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Export with
files (e.g. images/video frames)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>dicom_to_nifti</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Convert
DICOM images to NIfTI. Applicable when with_files is True.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>png</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Export labels as
PNG masks.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>rt_struct</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Export
labels as DICOM RT-Struct. (Only for DICOM images)</p></li>
<li><p><strong>mhd</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Export
segmentation masks in MHD format.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>destination</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Destination directory (Default: current directory)</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>Datapoint and labels in RedBrick AI format. See <a
href="https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#export"
class="reference external">https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#export</a></p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>Iterator[<a href="formats/index.html#redbrick.types.task.OutputTask"
class="reference internal" title="redbrick.types.task.OutputTask"><span
class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">OutputTask</code></span></a>]</p>
</dd>
</dl>
<div class="admonition note">
<p>Note</p>
<p>If both semantic_mask and binary_mask options are True, then one
binary mask will be generated per class.</p>
</div>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">list_tasks</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">search</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">TaskFilters.ALL</span></span></em>, <em><span
class="n"><span class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span
class="o"><span class="pre">=</span></span><span
class="default_value"><span class="pre">10</span></span></em>, <em><span
class="n"><span class="pre">limit</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">50</span></span></em>, <em><span class="o"><span
class="pre">*</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">stage_name</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">user_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">task_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">task_name</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">exact_match</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">completed_at</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/export.html#Export.list_tasks"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.export.Export.list_tasks" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Search tasks based on multiple queries for a project. This function
returns minimal meta-data about the queried tasks.</p>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; project = redbrick.get_project(org_id, project_id, api_key, url)
&gt;&gt;&gt; result = project.export.list_tasks()</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>search</strong> (<a href="#redbrick.TaskFilters"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.common.enums.TaskFilters"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">TaskFilters</code></span></a> =
TaskFilters.ALL) – Task filter type.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 10</em>) – The number of
requests that will be made in parallel.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>limit</strong> (<em>Optional[int]</em> <em>= 50</em>) –
The number of tasks to return. Use None to return all tasks matching the
search query.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>stage_name</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) –</p>
<dl>
<dt>If present, will return tasks that are:</dt>
<dd>
<ol>
<li><p>Available in stage_name: If search == TaskFilters.QUEUED</p></li>
<li><p>Completed in stage_name: If search ==
TaskFilters.COMPLETED</p></li>
</ol>
</dd>
</dl></li>
<li><p><strong>user_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>= None</em>)
–</p>
<dl>
<dt>User id/email. If present, will return tasks that are:</dt>
<dd>
<ol>
<li><p>Assigned to user_id: If search == TaskFilters.QUEUED</p></li>
<li><p>Completed by user_id: If search == TaskFilters.COMPLETED</p></li>
</ol>
</dd>
</dl></li>
<li><p><strong>task_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>= None</em>)
– If present, will return data for the given task id.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>task_name</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – If present, will return data for the given task name. This
will do a prefix search with the given task name.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>exact_match</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Applicable
when searching for tasks by task_name. If True, will do a full match
instead of partial match.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>completed_at</strong>
(<em>Optional[Tuple[Optional[float],</em> <em>Optional[float]]]</em>
<em>= None</em>) – If present, will return tasks that were completed in
the given time range. The tuple contains the from and to timestamps
respectively.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; [{
    &quot;taskId&quot;: str,
    &quot;name&quot;: str,
    &quot;createdAt&quot;: str,
    &quot;updatedAt&quot;: str,
    &quot;currentStageName&quot;: str,
    &quot;createdBy&quot;?: {&quot;userId&quot;: str, &quot;email&quot;: str},
    &quot;priority&quot;?: float([0, 1]),
    &quot;metaData&quot;?: dict,
    &quot;series&quot;?: [{&quot;name&quot;?: str, &quot;metaData&quot;?: dict}],
    &quot;assignees&quot;?: [{
        &quot;user&quot;: str,
        &quot;status&quot;: TaskStates,
        &quot;assignedAt&quot;: datetime,
        &quot;lastSavedAt&quot;?: datetime,
        &quot;completedAt&quot;?: datetime,
        &quot;timeSpentMs&quot;?: float,
    }]
}]</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>Iterator[Dict]</p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">get_task_events</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="o"><span
class="pre">*</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">task_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">only_ground_truth</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">True</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">10</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">from_timestamp</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">with_labels</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/export.html#Export.get_task_events"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.export.Export.get_task_events" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Generate an audit log of all actions performed on tasks.</p>
<p>Use this method to get a detailed summary of all the actions
performed on your tasks, including:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>Who uploaded the data</p></li>
<li><p>Who annotated your tasks</p></li>
<li><p>Who reviewed your tasks</p></li>
<li><p>and more.</p></li>
</ul>
<p>This can be particulary useful to present to auditors who are
interested in your quality control workflows.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>task_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>= None</em>)
– If set, returns events only for the given task.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>only_ground_truth</strong> (<em>bool = True</em>) – If
set to True, will return events for tasks that have been completed in
your workflow.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 10</em>) – The number of
requests that will be made in parallel.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>from_timestamp</strong> (<em>Optional[float]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – If the timestamp is mentioned, will only export tasks that
were labeled/updated since the given timestamp. Format - output from
datetime.timestamp()</p></li>
<li><p><strong>with_labels</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Get
metadata of labels submitted in each stage.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; [{
    &quot;taskId&quot;: string,
    &quot;currentStageName&quot;: string,
    &quot;events&quot;: List[Dict]
}]</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>Iterator[Dict]</p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">get_active_time</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="o"><span
class="pre">*</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">stage_name</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">task_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">100</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a

href="#redbrick.common.export.Export.get_active_time" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>

<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>

return the time info.</p></li>

– If set, will return info for the given task in the given

size.</p></li>

<dd>
<p>Bases: <span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">ABC</code></span></p>
<p>Primary interface for uploading to a project.</p>
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; project = redbrick.get_project(api_key=&quot;&quot;, org_id=&quot;&quot;, project_id=&quot;&quot;)
&gt;&gt;&gt; project.upload</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">create_datapoints</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">storage_id</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">points</span></span></em>, <em><span class="o"><span
class="pre">*</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">is_ground_truth</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">segmentation_mapping</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">rt_struct</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">mhd</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">label_storage_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">label_validate</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">prune_segmentations</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">50</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/upload.html#Upload.create_datapoints"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.upload.Upload.create_datapoints"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Create datapoints in project.</p>
<p>Upload data, and optionally annotations, to your project. Please
visit <a href="https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#import"
class="reference external">our documentation</a> to understand the
format for <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">points</code></span>.</p>
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>project = redbrick.get_project(org_id, project_id, api_key, url)
points = [
    {
        &quot;name&quot;: &quot;...&quot;,
        &quot;series&quot;: [
            {
                &quot;items&quot;: &quot;...&quot;,

                # These fields are needed for importing segmentations.
                &quot;segmentations&quot;: &quot;...&quot;,
                &quot;segmentMap&quot;: {...}
            }
        ]
    }
]
project.upload.create_datapoints(storage_id, points)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>storage_id</strong> (<em>str</em>) – Your RedBrick AI
external storage_id. This can be found under the Storage Tab on the
RedBrick AI platform. To directly upload images to rbai, use
redbrick.StorageMethod.REDBRICK.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>points</strong> (List[<a
href="formats/index.html#redbrick.types.task.InputTask"
class="reference internal" title="redbrick.types.task.InputTask"><span
class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">InputTask</code></span></a>]) – Please see the
RedBrick AI reference documentation for overview of the format. <a
href="https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#import"
class="reference external">https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#import</a>.
All the fields with annotation information are optional.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>is_ground_truth</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – If
labels are provided in <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">points</code></span>, and this
parameters is set to true, the labels will be added to the Ground Truth
stage.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>segmentation_mapping</strong> (<em>Optional[Dict]</em>
<em>= None</em>) – Optional mapping of semantic_mask segmentation class
ids and RedBrick categories.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>rt_struct</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Upload
segmentations from DICOM RT-Struct files.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>mhd</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Upload
segmentations from MHD files.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>label_storage_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Optional label storage id to reference nifti segmentations.
Defaults to items storage_id if not specified.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>label_validate</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) –
Validate label nifti instances and segment map.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>prune_segmentations</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) –
Prune segmentations that are not part of the series.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 50</em>) –</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>List of task objects with key response if successful, else error</p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>List[Dict]</p>
</dd>
</dl>
<div class="admonition note">
<p>Note</p>
<p>1. If doing direct upload, please use <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">redbrick.StorageMethod.REDBRICK</code></span>
as the storage id. Your items path must be a valid path to a locally
stored image.</p>
<p>2. When doing direct upload i.e. <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">redbrick.StorageMethod.REDBRICK</code></span>,
if you didn’t specify a “name” field in your datapoints object, we will
assign the “items” path to it.</p>
</div>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>

<dd>
<p>Update tasks labels at any point in project pipeline.</p>
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>project = redbrick.get_project(...)
tasks = [
    {
        &quot;taskId&quot;: &quot;...&quot;,
        &quot;series&quot;: [{...}]
    },
]

# Overwrite labels in tasks
project.upload.update_tasks_labels(tasks)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>points</strong> (List[<a
href="formats/index.html#redbrick.types.task.OutputTask"
class="reference internal" title="redbrick.types.task.OutputTask"><span
class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">OutputTask</code></span></a>]) – Please see
the RedBrick AI reference documentation for overview of the format. <a
href="https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#export"
class="reference external">https://sdk.redbrickai.com/formats/index.html#export</a>.
All the fields with annotation information are optional.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>rt_struct</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Upload
segmentations from DICOM RT-Struct files.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>mhd</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Upload
segmentations from MHD files.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>label_storage_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Optional label storage id to reference nifti segmentations.
Defaults to project annnotation storage_id if not specified.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>label_validate</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) –
Validate label nifti instances and segment map.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>prune_segmentations</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) –
Prune segmentations that are not part of the series.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 50</em>) –</p></li>
<li><p><strong>finalize</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Submit the
task in current stage.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>time_spent_ms</strong> (<em>Optional[int]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Time spent on the task in milliseconds.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>extra_data</strong> (<em>Optional[Dict]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Extra data to be stored along with the task.</p></li>
</ul>

<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">send_tasks_to_stage</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">task_ids</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">stage_name</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">50</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/upload.html#Upload.send_tasks_to_stage"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.upload.Upload.send_tasks_to_stage"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Send tasks to different stage.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>task_ids</strong> (<em>List[str]</em>) – List of tasks to
move.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>stage_name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – The stage to which
you want to move the tasks. Use “END” to move tasks to ground
truth.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 50</em>) – Batch size per
request.</p></li>
