<h2 id="labeling">Labeling<a href="#labeling" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this heading">#</a></h2>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-prename descclassname"><span
class="pre">redbrick.common.labeling.</span></span><span
class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">Labeling</span></span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/labeling.html#Labeling"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.labeling.Labeling" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Bases: <span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">ABC</code></span></p>
<p>Perform programmatic labeling and review tasks.</p>
<p>The Labeling class allows you to programmatically submit tasks. This
can be useful for times when you want to make bulk actions e.g accepting
several tasks, or make automated actions like using automated methods
for review.</p>
<div class="admonition-information admonition">
<p>Information</p>
<p>The Labeling module provides several methods to query tasks and
assign tasks to different users. Refer to this section for guidance on
when to use each method:</p>
<ul>
<li><p><a href="#redbrick.common.labeling.Labeling.assign_tasks"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.common.labeling.Labeling.assign_tasks"><span
class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">assign_tasks</code></span></a>. Use this
method when you already have the <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">task_ids</code></span> you want to
assign to a particular user. If you don’t have the <span
class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">task_ids</code></span>, you can
query the tasks using <a
href="#redbrick.common.export.Export.list_tasks"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.common.export.Export.list_tasks"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">list_tasks</code></span></a>.</p></li>
</ul>
</div>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">put_tasks</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">stage_name</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">tasks</span></span></em>, <em><span class="o"><span
class="pre">*</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">finalize</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">True</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">existing_labels</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">rt_struct</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">mhd</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">review_result</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">label_storage_id</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">'22222222-2222-2222-2222-222222222222'</span></span></em>,
<em><span class="n"><span class="pre">label_validate</span></span><span
class="o"><span class="pre">=</span></span><span
class="default_value"><span class="pre">False</span></span></em>,
<em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">prune_segmentations</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">False</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">concurrency</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">50</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/labeling.html#Labeling.put_tasks"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.labeling.Labeling.put_tasks" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Put tasks with new labels or a review result.</p>
<p>Use this method to programmatically submit tasks with labels in Label
stage, or to programmatically accept/reject/correct tasks in a Review
stage. If you don’t already have a list of <span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">task_id</code></span>, you can use
<a href="#redbrick.common.export.Export.list_tasks"
class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.common.export.Export.list_tasks"><span class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">list_tasks</code></span></a> to get a filtered
list of tasks in your project, that you want to work upon.</p>
<div class="tab-set docutils">
Label
<div class="tab-content docutils">
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>project = redbrick.get_project(...)
tasks = [
    {
        &quot;taskId&quot;: &quot;...&quot;,
        &quot;series&quot;: [{...}]
    },
]

# Submit tasks with new labels
project.labeling.put_tasks(&quot;Label&quot;, tasks)

# Save tasks with new labels, without submitting
project.labeling.put_tasks(&quot;Label&quot;, tasks, finalize=False)

# Submit tasks with existing labels
project.labeling.put_tasks(&quot;Label&quot;, [{&quot;taskId&quot;:&quot;...&quot;}], existing_labels=True)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
</div>
Review
<div class="tab-content docutils">
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>project = redbrick.get_project(...)

# Set review_result to True if you want to accept the tasks
project.review.put_tasks(&quot;Review_1&quot;, [{taskId: &quot;...&quot;}], review_result=True)

# Set review_result to False if you want to reject the tasks
project.review.put_tasks(&quot;Review_1&quot;, [{taskId: &quot;...&quot;}], review_result=False)

# Add labels if you want to accept the tasks with correction
project.review.put_tasks(&quot;Review_1&quot;, [{taskId: &quot;...&quot;, series: [{...}]}])</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>stage_name</strong> (<em>str</em>) – The stage to which
you want to submit the tasks. This must be the same stage as which you
called get_tasks on.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>tasks</strong> (List[<a
href="formats/index.html#redbrick.types.task.OutputTask"
class="reference internal" title="redbrick.types.task.OutputTask"><span
class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">OutputTask</code></span></a>]) – Tasks with
new labels or review result.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>finalize</strong> (<em>bool = True</em>) – Finalize the
task. If you want to save the task without submitting, set this to
False.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>existing_labels</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – If
True, the tasks will be submitted with their existing labels. Applies
only to Label stage.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>rt_struct</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Upload
segmentations from DICOM RT-Struct files.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>mhd</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) – Upload
segmentations from MHD files.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>review_result</strong> (<em>Optional[bool]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Accepts or rejects the task based on the boolean value.
Applies only to Review stage.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>label_storage_id</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Optional label storage id to reference external nifti
segmentations. Defaults to project settings’ annotation storage_id if
not specified.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>label_validate</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) –
Validate label nifti instances and segment map.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>prune_segmentations</strong> (<em>bool = False</em>) –
Prune segmentations that are not part of the series.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>concurrency</strong> (<em>int = 50</em>) –</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>A list of tasks that failed.</p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>List[<a href="formats/index.html#redbrick.types.task.OutputTask"
class="reference internal" title="redbrick.types.task.OutputTask"><span
class="pre"><code
class="sourceCode python">OutputTask</code></span></a>]</p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">assign_tasks</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">task_ids</span></span></em>, <em><span class="o"><span
class="pre">*</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">email</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">emails</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">None</span></span></em>, <em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">refresh</span></span><span class="o"><span
class="pre">=</span></span><span class="default_value"><span
class="pre">True</span></span></em><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/labeling.html#Labeling.assign_tasks"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.labeling.Labeling.assign_tasks"
class="headerlink" title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Assign tasks to specified email or current API key.</p>
<p>Unassigns all users from the task if neither of the <span
class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">email</code></span> or <span
class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">current_user</code></span> are
set.</p>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; project = redbrick.get_project(org_id, project_id, api_key)
&gt;&gt;&gt; project.labeling.assign_tasks([task_id], email=email)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>task_ids</strong> (<em>List[str]</em>) – List of unique
<span class="pre"><code
class="docutils literal notranslate">task_id</code></span> of the tasks
you want to assign.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>email</strong> (<em>Optional[str]</em> <em>= None</em>) –
The email of the user you want to assign this task to. Make sure the
user has adequate permissions to be assigned this task in the
project.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>emails</strong> (<em>Optional[List[str]]</em> <em>=
None</em>) – Used for projects with Consensus activated. The emails of
the users you want to assign this task to. Make sure the users have
adequate permissions to be assigned this task in the project.</p></li>
<li><p><strong>refresh</strong> (<em>bool = True</em>) – Used for
projects with Consensus activated. If True, will overwrite the
assignment to the current users.</p></li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>Returns<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<dl>
<dt>List of affected tasks.</dt>
<dd>
<div class="doctest highlight-default notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; [{&quot;taskId&quot;, &quot;name&quot;, &quot;stageName&quot;}]</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p>List[Dict]</p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">

<h2 id="workforce">Workforce<a href="#workforce" class="headerlink"

<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">class</span><span class="w"> </span></em><span
class="sig-prename descclassname"><span
class="pre">redbrick.common.member.</span></span><span
class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">Workforce</span></span><a

<dd>
<p>Bases: <span class="pre"><code

<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">get_member</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><em><span class="n"><span
class="pre">member_id</span></span></em><span
class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/member.html#Workforce.get_member"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.member.Workforce.get_member" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Get a project member.</p>
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>project = redbrick.get_project(org_id, project_id, api_key)
member = project.workforce.get_member(member_id)</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Parameters<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p><strong>member_id</strong> (<em>str</em>) – Unique member userId or
email.</p>
</dd>
<dt>Return type<span class="colon">:</span></dt>
<dd>
<p><a href="#redbrick.ProjectMember" class="reference internal"
title="redbrick.common.member.ProjectMember">ProjectMember</a></p>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><em><span class="pre">abstract</span><span class="w">
</span></em><span class="sig-name descname"><span
class="pre">list_members</span></span><span
class="sig-paren">(</span><span class="sig-paren">)</span><a
href="_modules/redbrick/common/member.html#Workforce.list_members"
class="reference internal"><span class="viewcode-link"><span
class="pre">[source]</span></span></a><a
href="#redbrick.common.member.Workforce.list_members" class="headerlink"
title="Link to this definition">#</a></dt>
<dd>
<p>Get a list of all project members.</p>
<div class="highlight-python notranslate">
<div class="highlight">
<pre><code>project = redbrick.get_project(org_id, project_id, api_key)
members = project.workforce.list_members()</code></pre>
</div>
</div>

</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
